    37 function extractWeekday(text: string): { value: string; type: 'fixed' } | null {
    38   const match = text.match(/周[\s]*([一二三四五六日天1-6])/);
    39   if (match) {
    40     const ch = match[1];
    41     return { value: wMap[ch] || ch, type: 'fixed' };
    42   }

    44   if (match2) {
    45     const ch = match2[1];
    46     return { value: wMap[ch] || ch, type: 'fixed' };
    47   }
    48   const match3 = text.match(/\b([0-6])\b/);

    51   }

    53 }

    55 function extractDate(text: string): { value: string; type: 'temporary' } | null {
    56   const match = text.match(/(\d{4}[\-/]\d{1,2}[\-/]\d{1,2})/);
    57   if (match) {
    58     return { value: match[1].replace(/\//g, '-'), type: 'temporary' };
    59   }
    60   return null;
    61 }

    63 function extractTime(text: string): { start: string; end: string } | null {
    64   const match = text.match(/(\d{1,2}:\d{2})\s*[-~—到至]+\s*(\d{1,2}:\d{2})/);
    65   if (match) {
    66     return { start: match[1], end: match[2] };
    67   }
    68   const single = text.match(/(\d{1,2}:\d{2})/);
    69   if (single) {
    70     return { start: single[1], end: '23:00' };
    71   }
    72   return null;
    73 }

```
      return h < 6 ? `z${t}` : `a${t}`;
    };
    return [...generic, ...specific].sort((a, b) => sortKey(a.start_time).localeCompare(sortKey(b.start_time)));
  }, [activeDateObj, sessionMap]);

  // Desktop calendar: all unique sessions and per-date sessions
  const allSessions = useMemo(() => {
    const seen = new Set<string>();
    const list: BarSession[] = [];
    Object.values(sessionMap).flat().forEach((s) => {
      if (!seen.has(s.id)) {
        seen.add(s.id);
        list.push(s);
      }
    });
    const sortKey = (t: string | null) => {
      if (!t) return '';
      const h = parseInt(t.slice(0, 2));
      return h < 6 ? `z${t}` : `a${t}`;
    };
    return list.sort((a, b) => sortKey(a.start_time).localeCompare(sortKey(b.start_time)));
  }, [sessionMap]);

  const getDaySessions = (dateStr: string) => {
    const d = new Date(dateStr + 'T00:00:00');
    const wd = d.getDay();
    const generic = sessionMap['generic'] || [];
    const specific = sessionMap[wd] || [];
    const sortKey = (t: string | null) => {
      if (!t) return '';
      const h = parseInt(t.slice(0, 2));
      return h < 6 ? `z${t}` : `a${t}`;
    };
    return [...generic, ...specific].sort((a, b) => sortKey(a.start_time).localeCompare(sortKey(b.start_time)));
  };
```

   282 export async function updateAvailability(id: string, updates: Partial<ArtistAvailability>): Promise<void> {

```
            {/* 固定档期：只显示星期 */}
            {availForm.availability_type === 'fixed' && (
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <Label>星期</Label>
                <Select value={String(availForm.day_of_week ?? 0)} onValueChange={(v) => setAvailForm({ ...availForm, day_of_week: parseInt(v) })}>
                  <SelectTrigger className="h-11"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
                  <SelectContent>

              </div>
            )}

            {availForm.availability_type === 'temporary' && (
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label>具体日期（精确到某一天，留空则使用下方星期）</Label>
                  <Input type="date" className="h-11" value={availForm.specific_date || ''} onChange={(e) => {
```

New String: ```
  function openBatchEdit() {
    const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    // Check same artist
    const artistsInSelection = new Set(selected.map((a) => a.artist_id));
    if (artistsInSelection.size > 1) {
      toast.error('批量编辑只能针对同一个歌手');
      return;
    }

    // Compute common values
    const allSame = (key: keyof ArtistAvailability) => {
      const vals = selected.map((s) => s[key]);
      return vals.every((v) => v === vals[0]) ? vals[0] : undefined;
    };

    const typeVal = allSame('availability_type');
    const dowVal = allSame('day_of_week');
    const dateVal = allSame('specific_date');
    const startVal = allSame('available_start');
    const endVal = allSame('available_end');
    const availVal = allSame('is_available');
    const noteVal = allSame('note');

    setBatchEditForm({
      availability_type: typeVal || '',
      day_of_week: dowVal !== undefined ? dowVal : null,
      specific_date: dateVal ? dateVal.split('T')[0] : '',
      available_start: startVal || '',
      available_end: endVal || '',
      is_available: availVal !== undefined ? availVal : null,
      note: noteVal || '',
    });
    setBatchEditFields(new Set());
    setBatchEditOpen(true);
  }

  async function saveBatchEdit() {
    const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    try {
      for (const a of selected) {
        const updates: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {};
        if (batchEditFields.has('availability_type')) {
          updates.availability_type = batchEditForm.availability_type as 'fixed' | 'temporary';
          if (updates.availability_type === 'fixed') {
            updates.specific_date = null;
          }
        }
        if (batchEditFields.has('day_of_week')) updates.day_of_week = batchEditForm.day_of_week;
        if (batchEditFields.has('specific_date')) {
          updates.specific_date = batchEditForm.specific_date || null;
          if (batchEditForm.specific_date) updates.day_of_week = null;
        }
        if (batchEditFields.has('available_start')) updates.available_start = batchEditForm.available_start || null;
        if (batchEditFields.has('available_end')) updates.available_end = batchEditForm.available_end || null;
        if (batchEditFields.has('is_available')) updates.is_available = batchEditForm.is_available!;
        if (batchEditFields.has('note')) updates.note = batchEditForm.note || null;
        if (Object.keys(updates).length > 0) {
          await updateAvailability(a.id, updates);
        }
      }
      toast.success(`已更新 ${selected.length} 条档期`);
      setBatchEditOpen(false);
      setSelectedIds(new Set());
      loadData();
    } catch (e: any) {
      toast.error('批量更新失败：' + e.message);
    }
  }
```

   438   async function saveAvailability() {
   439     if (!dialogArtistId) {
   440       toast.error('请选择歌手');
   441       return;
   442     }
   443     const payload: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {
   444       ...availForm,
   445       artist_id: dialogArtistId,
   446     };
   447     if (availForm.availability_type === 'fixed') {
   448       payload.specific_date = null;
   449     } else {
   450       // temporary: 如果填了具体日期就用日期，否则用星期

   468       loadData();

```
        const updates: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {};

```
New String: ```
  async function saveBatchEdit() {
    const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    const first = selected[0];
    const artistId = first.artist_id;
    const existingDays = new Set<number>();
    selected.forEach((s) => {
      if (s.day_of_week !== null && s.day_of_week !== undefined) existingDays.add(s.day_of_week);
    });

    try {
      // 1. 删除取消勾选的星期
      for (const day of existingDays) {
        if (!batchEditWeekDays.has(day)) {
          const toDelete = selected.find((s) => s.day_of_week === day);
          if (toDelete) await deleteAvailability(toDelete.id);
        }
      }

      // 2. 更新保留的档期（如果勾选了其他字段）
      for (const day of batchEditWeekDays) {
        const record = selected.find((s) => s.day_of_week === day);
        if (record && batchEditFields.size > 0) {
          const updates: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {};
          if (batchEditFields.has('availability_type')) {
            updates.availability_type = batchEditForm.availability_type as 'fixed' | 'temporary';
            if (updates.availability_type === 'fixed') updates.specific_date = null;
          }
          if (batchEditFields.has('available_start')) updates.available_start = batchEditForm.available_start || null;
          if (batchEditFields.has('available_end')) updates.available_end = batchEditForm.available_end || null;
          if (batchEditFields.has('is_available')) updates.is_available = batchEditForm.is_available!;
          if (batchEditFields.has('note')) updates.note = batchEditForm.note || null;
          if (Object.keys(updates).length > 0) {
            await updateAvailability(record.id, updates);
          }
        }
      }

      // 3. 创建新勾选的星期
      for (const day of batchEditWeekDays) {
        if (!existingDays.has(day)) {
          const payload: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {
            artist_id: artistId,
            availability_type: (batchEditForm.availability_type as 'fixed' | 'temporary') || first.availability_type,
            day_of_week: day,
            specific_date: null,
            available_start: batchEditFields.has('available_start') ? (batchEditForm.available_start || null) : (first.available_start || '20:00'),
            available_end: batchEditFields.has('available_end') ? (batchEditForm.available_end || null) : (first.available_end || '23:00'),
            is_available: batchEditFields.has('is_available') ? batchEditForm.is_available! : first.is_available,
            note: batchEditFields.has('note') ? (batchEditForm.note || null) : first.note,
          };
          await createAvailability(payload as any);
        }
      }

      toast.success('批量更新完成');
      setBatchEditOpen(false);
      setSelectedIds(new Set());
      loadData();
    } catch (e: any) {
      toast.error('批量更新失败：' + e.message);
    }
  }
```

   358   function openBatchEdit(artistId?: string) {
   359     const selected = artistId
   360       ? availabilities.filter((a) => a.artist_id === artistId)

   373       const vals = selected.map((s) => s[key]);

   412   async function saveBatchEdit() {
   413     const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
   414     if (selected.length === 0) return;
   415 
   416     const first = selected[0];
   417     const artistId = first.artist_id;

New String: ```
  function openBatchEdit(artistId?: string) {
    const selected = artistId
      ? availabilities.filter((a) => a.artist_id === artistId)
      : availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    // Check same artist
    const artistsInSelection = new Set(selected.map((a) => a.artist_id));
    if (artistsInSelection.size > 1) {
      toast.error('批量编辑只能针对同一个歌手');
      return;
    }

    // 如果是通过歌手卡片调用的，设置 selectedIds 为该歌手所有档期
    if (artistId) {
      setSelectedIds(new Set(selected.map((s) => s.id)));
    }

    // Compute common values
```

     1 import type { Artist, ArtistAvailability, BarSession } from '@/types/types';
     2 
     3 const ALL_STYLES = ['R&B', '流行', '英文', '唱跳', '气氛', '抒情', '说唱'];
     4 export { ALL_STYLES };
     5 
     6 function timeToMinutes(t: string): number {
     7   const [h, m] = t.split(':').map(Number);
     8   return h * 60 + m;
     9 }
    10 
    11 /**
    12  * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
    13  * 逻辑：节的开始时间必须在歌手可排范围内（歌手到场后 + 离场前30分钟缓冲）
    14  * 例如歌手21:30-23:00 → 有效到23:30，第3节23:30开始也能排
    15  */
    16 function canCoverSession(
    17   availStart: string,
    18   availEnd: string,
    19   sessionStart: string,
    20   _sessionEnd: string
    21 ): boolean {
    22   // 歌手来得比节开始还晚 → 不能排
    23   if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;
    24 
    25   // 给歌手结束时间加30分钟缓冲（离场/过渡时间）
    26   const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd) + 30;
    27   const sessionStartMin = timeToMinutes(sessionStart);
    28 
    29   return availEndMin >= sessionStartMin;
    30 }
    31 
    32 export function isArtistAvailable(
    33   artist: Artist,
    34   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
    35   date: Date,
    36   session: BarSession
    37 ): boolean {
    38   const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    39   const dayOfWeek = date.getDay();
    40 
    41   // 1. Check temporary with specific_date (exact date override, highest priority)
    42   const tempExact = availabilities.find(
    43     (a) =>
    44       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    45       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    46       a.specific_date === dateStr
    47   );
    48   if (tempExact) {
    49     if (!tempExact.is_available) return false;
    50     if (
    51       !tempExact.available_start ||
    52       !tempExact.available_end ||
    53       !session.start_time ||
    54       !session.end_time
    55     ) {
    56       return true;
    57     }
    58     return canCoverSession(
    59       tempExact.available_start,
    60       tempExact.available_end,
    61       session.start_time,
    62       session.end_time
    63     );
    64   }
    65 
    66   // 2. Check temporary with day_of_week (weekly temporary schedule)
    67   const tempWeekly = availabilities.find(
    68     (a) =>
    69       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    70       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    71       a.specific_date === null &&
    72       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
    73   );
    74   if (tempWeekly) {
    75     if (!tempWeekly.is_available) return false;
    76     if (
    77       !tempWeekly.available_start ||
    78       !tempWeekly.available_end ||
    79       !session.start_time ||
    80       !session.end_time
    81     ) {
    82       return true;
    83     }
    84     return canCoverSession(
    85       tempWeekly.available_start,
    86       tempWeekly.available_end,
    87       session.start_time,
    88       session.end_time
    89     );
    90   }
    91 
    92   // 3. Check fixed schedule
    93   const fixedAvail = availabilities.find(
    94     (a) =>
    95       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    96       a.availability_type === 'fixed' &&
    97       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
    98   );
    99 
   100   if (!fixedAvail) return false;

   124 export function hasFixedAvailability(
   125   artistId: string,
   126   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   127   dayOfWeek: number
   128 ): boolean {
   129   return availabilities.some(
   130     (a) =>
   131       a.artist_id === artistId &&
   132       a.availability_type === 'fixed' &&
   133       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek &&
   134       a.is_available
   135   );
   136 }
   137 
   138 /**
   139  * Filter available artists by style priority (degradation)
   140  * style_tags array order = priority order
   141  * e.g. [抒情, R&B, 说唱] → first try 抒情-only, then R&B-only, then 说唱-only
   142  * Returns: matched in priority order, unmatched (available but no style match), priorityGroups
   143  */
   144 export function filterAndSortArtists(
   145   artists: Artist[],
   146   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   147   date: Date,
   148   session: BarSession,
   149   requiredStyles: string[]
   150 ): { matched: Artist[]; unmatched: Artist[]; priorityGroups: Artist[][] } {
   151   const allAvailable = artists.filter((a) =>
   152     isArtistAvailable(a, availabilities, date, session)
   153   );
   154 
   155   if (requiredStyles.length === 0) {
   156     return {
   157       matched: allAvailable,
   158       unmatched: [],
   159       priorityGroups: [allAvailable],
   160     };
   161   }
   162 
   163   const pickedIds = new Set<string>();
   164   const priorityGroups: Artist[][] = [];
   165   const allMatched: Artist[] = [];
   166 
   167   for (const style of requiredStyles) {
   168     const matches = allAvailable.filter(
   169       (a) => !pickedIds.has(a.id) && a.style_tags.includes(style)
   170     );
   171     priorityGroups.push(matches);
   172     for (const a of matches) {
   173       allMatched.push(a);
   174       pickedIds.add(a.id);
   175     }
   176   }
   177 
   178   const unmatched = allAvailable.filter((a) => !pickedIds.has(a.id));
   179 
   180   return { matched: allMatched, unmatched, priorityGroups };
   181 }
   182 
   183 // For auto-assign: return style-matched available artists in priority order
   184 export function filterStyleMatchedArtists(
   185   artists: Artist[],
   186   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   187   date: Date,
   188   session: BarSession,
   189   requiredStyles: string[]
   190 ): Artist[] {
   191   const { matched } = filterAndSortArtists(
   192     artists,
   193     availabilities,
   194     date,
   195     session,
   196     requiredStyles
   197   );
   198   return matched;
   199 }

    98 export async function getBarSessions(barId: string, weekday?: number): Promise<BarSession[]> {
    99   let q = supabase.from('bar_sessions').select('*').eq('bar_id', barId).order('session_number');
   100   if (weekday !== undefined) {
   101     q = q.eq('weekday', weekday);
   102   } else {
   103     // Return both weekday-specific and null (generic) when no weekday filter
   104     // Actually for the full list view we want all, but for schedule generation we want a specific weekday
   105   }
   106   const { data, error } = await q;
   107   if (error) throw error;
   108   return Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
   109 }
   110 
   111 export async function getBarSessionsForDate(barId: string, weekday: number): Promise<BarSession[]> {
   112   // First try weekday-specific config
   113   const { data: specific, error: err1 } = await supabase
   114     .from('bar_sessions')
   115     .select('*')
   116     .eq('bar_id', barId)
   117     .eq('weekday', weekday)
   118     .order('session_number');
   119   if (err1) throw err1;
   120   if (specific && specific.length > 0) return specific;
   121   // Fallback to generic config (weekday is null)
   122   const { data: generic, error: err2 } = await supabase
   123     .from('bar_sessions')
   124     .select('*')
   125     .eq('bar_id', barId)
   126     .is('weekday', null)
   127     .order('session_number');
   128   if (err2) throw err2;
   129   return Array.isArray(generic) ? generic : [];
   130 }

AgentThinkAction(thought='找到核心bug了！\n\n`canCoverSession` 函数在处理跨天节次（如第4节 01:00-01:30）时有严重bug：\n\n- sessionStart = "01:00" → 60分钟\n- availEnd = "23:00" → 1380分钟\n- availEndMin = 1380 + 30 = 1410\n- 1410 >= 60 → true ❌\n\n但实际上23:00是当天晚上，01:00是次日凌晨。歌手23:00离场后不可能参加凌晨01:00的节次！\n\n这是因为 `timeToMinutes` 把01:00当作了当天的60分钟（实际上应该是次日凌晨），而23:00是1380分钟，所以23:00 > 01:00。\n\n修复方案：当 sessionStart < "06:00"（跨天凌晨节次）且 availEnd >= "12:00"（当天晚上离场），则不能覆盖。\n\n另外用户的第2个需求"所有档期匹配的歌手都要放进可选歌手里"——现在弹窗已经显示了 matched 和 unmatched 歌手，但可能因为时间匹配bug，某些歌手被错误地排除在 allAvailable 之外。修复时间匹配bug后，这些歌手就会正确出现了。', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bt7xab93905d/src/lib/schedule.ts]
Thought: 
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：节的开始时间必须在歌手可排范围内（歌手到场后 + 离场前30分钟缓冲）
 * 例如歌手21:30-23:00 → 有效到23:30，第3节23:30开始也能排
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  _sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 歌手来得比节开始还晚 → 不能排
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 给歌手结束时间加30分钟缓冲（离场/过渡时间）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd) + 30;
  const sessionStartMin = timeToMinutes(sessionStart);

  return availEndMin >= sessionStartMin;
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：节的开始时间必须在歌手可排范围内（歌手到场后 + 离场前30分钟缓冲）
 * 例如歌手21:30-23:00 → 有效到23:30，第3节23:30开始也能排
 * 
 * 跨天处理：节次在凌晨（如01:00）属于第二天，歌手当天晚上（如23:00）离场不能覆盖
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  _sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 歌手来得比节开始还晚 → 不能排
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 跨天节次检查：session 在凌晨（如01:00），但歌手是当天晚上（如23:00）
  // 这种情况下歌手已离场，不能覆盖次日凌晨节次
  if (sessionStart < '06:00' && availEnd >= '12:00') {
    return false;
  }

  // 给歌手结束时间加30分钟缓冲（离场/过渡时间）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd) + 30;
  const sessionStartMin = timeToMinutes(sessionStart);

  return availEndMin >= sessionStartMin;
}
```
